
.. _plugins_in_oracle.oci:

Oracle.Oci
==========

Collection version 4.20.0

.. toctree::
    :maxdepth: 1


Plugin Index
------------

These are the plugins in the oracle.oci collection


Inventory Plugins
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

* :ref:`oci <ansible_collections.oracle.oci.oci_inventory>` -- Oracle Cloud Infrastructure (OCI) inventory plugin
